account permissions of the user specified by user or domainuser the default is the permissions of the current logged on user on the computer issuing the command yes has to be used with s switch 00 00 00 00 00 getmac p specifies the password of the user account that is specified in the u parameter yes has to be used with s and u switches 00 00 00 00 00 getmac fo table l list l csv specifies the
